<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> (4148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">cley</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">clǣġ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klajjaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gley-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to glue, paste, stick together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klei.html>klei</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></span><span annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γλία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, lang="uk">ґлей</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glej</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related also to <span class="Latn" lang="en">clag</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">clog</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">clays</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mineral substance made up of small <a href = vnd.unilang:crystals.html>crystals</a> of silica and alumina, that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ductile when moist; the material of pre-fired ceramics.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1914</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Louis_Joseph_Vance" class="extiw" title="w:Louis Joseph Vance"><a href = vnd.unilang:louis.html>Louis</a> Joseph Vance</a>,  chapter I, in  <cite>Nobody</cite>, New York, N.Y. |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_H._Doran_Company" class="extiw" title="w:George H. Doran Company">George H[enry] Doran Company</a>, published 1915, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/40817384">40817384</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>Three chairs of the steamer type, all maimed, comprised the furniture of this roof-garden, with (by way of local colour) on one of the copings a row of four red <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></b> flower-pots filled with sun-baked dust<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>An earth material with ductile qualities.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">tennis</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tennis court surface made of crushed stone, brick, shale, or other unbound mineral aggregate.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The French Open <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> played on <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biblical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The material of the human body.
<ul><li><b>1611</b>, <i>Old <a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>Testament</a></i>, King James Version, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Job" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Book of Job">Job</a> 10:8-9:
<dl><dd>Thine hands have made <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> and fashioned <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> together round about...thou hast made <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> as the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1611</b>, <i>Old <a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>Testament</a></i>, King James Version, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Isaiah" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Book of Isaiah">Isaiah</a> 64:8:
<dl><dd>But now, <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> Lord, thou art our Father; <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> are the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></b>, and thou art our potter; and <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> are the work of thy hand.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A particle less than 3.9 microns in diameter, following the Wentworth scale.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> pipe for smoking tobacco.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">firearms<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> pigeon.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> shooting <b>clays</b> at the <a href = vnd.unilang:weekend.html>weekend</a>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>Land</a> or territory of a country or other political region, especially when subject to territorial claims
<dl><dd><i>Danzig <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> rightfully German <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">clays</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">claying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">clayed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To add <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> to, to spread <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> onto.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of sugar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To purify using <a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a>.
<ul><li><b>1776</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adam_Smith" class="extiw" title="w:Adam Smith"><a href = vnd.unilang:adam.html>Adam</a> Smith</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Wealth_of_Nations/Book_IV/Chapter_7" class="extiw" title="s:The Wealth of Nations/Book IV/Chapter 7">An Inquiry into the Nature and Causes of the Wealth of Nations</a></i>, Book IV, Chapter 7: Of Colonies, Part 2: Causes of Prosperity of New Colonies,
<dl><dd>They amounted, therefore, to a prohibition, at first of <b>claying</b> or refining sugar for any foreign market, and at present of <b>claying</b> or refining it for the market, which <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> off, perhaps, more than nine-tenths of the whole produce.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1809</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jonathan.html>Jonathan</a> Williams, <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jstor.org/pss/1004773">On the Process of <b>Claying</b> Sugar</a></i>, in <i>Transactions of the American Philosophical Society</i>, Volume 6.</li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1985</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:stuart.html>Stuart</a> B. Schwartz,  <cite>Sugar Plantations in the Formation of Brazilian Society: Bahia, 1550-1835</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=InAVH-gPgdkCamp;pg=PA200amp;dq=%22clay%7Cclays%7Cclaying%7Cclayed+sugar%22amp;hl=enamp;ei=8sroTbfpEJCyuAOkwvS8Dwamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;resnum=5amp;sqi=2amp;ved=0CD8Q6AEwBAv=onepageamp;q=%22clay%7Cclays%7Cclaying%7Cclayed%20sugar%22amp;f=false">[1]</a></sup>, page 200:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The Portuguese <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> mastered the technique of <b>claying</b> sugar, and other European nations tried to learn the <a href = vnd.unilang:secrets.html>secrets</a> from them.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***cleave.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a> (94563)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">cleven</i>, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> strong verb <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">clēofan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to split, to separate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kleubaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*glewbʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut, to slice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:clive.html>clive</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klieven.html>klieven</a></i>, dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">klieben</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">klyva</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nynorsk" class="extiw" title="w:Nynorsk">Norwegian Nynorsk</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nn">kløyva</i>; also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γλύφω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glúphō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">carve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <br />
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaves.html>cleaves</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cleaving</b>, <i>simple past</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en">cleft</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en">clove</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en">cleaved</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en">clave</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cleft</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cloven</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cleaved</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To split or sever something with, or as if with, a sharp instrument.
<dl><dd><i>The wings <b>cleaved</b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:foggy.html>foggy</a> air.</i></dd>
<dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. Newly Translated out of the Originall Tongues: amp; with the Former Translations Diligently Compared and Reuised, by His Maiesties Speciall Comandement. Appointed to be Read in Churches.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_James_Version" class="extiw" title="w:King James Version">King James Version</a>), London |  <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Imprinted at London by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barker_(printer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barker (printer)">Robert Barker</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="printer to the Kings Most Excellent Maiestie.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/964384981">964384981</a></small>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Psalms" class="extiw" title="w:Psalms">Psalms</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.kingjamesbibleonline.org/1611_Psalms-Chapter-78/15">78:15</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hee.html>Hee</a> <b>claue</b> the rockes in the wildernes: and gaue them <a href = vnd.unilang:drinke.html>drinke</a> as out of the great depthes.</span></div></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1599–1602</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hamlet" class="extiw" title="w:Hamlet">The <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>Tragedie</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>Hamlet</a>, Prince of Denmarke</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act III, scene iv]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>Hamlet</a>, thou hast <b>cleft</b> my heart in twain.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mineralogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To break a single crystal (such as a gemstone or semiconductor wafer) along one of its more symmetrical crystallographic <a href = vnd.unilang:planes.html>planes</a> (often by impact), forming facets on the resulting pieces.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To make or accomplish by or as if by cutting.
<dl><dd><i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:truck.html>truck</a> <b>cleaved</b> a path through the ice.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To split (a complex molecule) into simpler <a href = vnd.unilang:molecules.html>molecules</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To split.
<dl><dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. Newly Translated out of the Originall Tongues: amp; with the Former Translations Diligently Compared and Reuised, by His Maiesties Speciall Comandement. Appointed to be Read in Churches.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_James_Version" class="extiw" title="w:King James Version">King James Version</a>), London |  <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Imprinted at London by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barker_(printer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barker (printer)">Robert Barker</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="printer to the Kings Most Excellent Maiestie.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/964384981">964384981</a></small>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Numbers" class="extiw" title="w:Book of Numbers">Numbers</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.kingjamesbibleonline.org/1611_Numbers-Chapter-16/31">16:31</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And it <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to <a href = vnd.unilang:passen.html>passe</a> as he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> made an ende of speaking all these <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>, that the ground <b>claue</b> asunder that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> vnder them:</span></div></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mineralogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of a crystal, to split along a natural plane of division.</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaves.html>cleaves</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>Flat</a>, smooth surface produced by cleavage, or any similar surface produced by similar techniques, as in glass.</li></ol>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cleft</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">cleven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cleofian</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klibāną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gleybʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaves.html>cleaves</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cleaving</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cleaved</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cling, adhere or stick fast to something; used with to or unto.
<dl><dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. <dd><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. ***cleaver.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cleaver.html>cleaver</a> (52194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">clevere</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Couperet_%C3%A0_d%C3%A9biter_les_lapins_03.jpg/220px-Couperet_%C3%A0_d%C3%A9biter_les_lapins_03.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Couperet_%C3%A0_d%C3%A9biter_les_lapins_03.jpg/330px-Couperet_%C3%A0_d%C3%A9biter_les_lapins_03.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Couperet_%C3%A0_d%C3%A9biter_les_lapins_03.jpg/440px-Couperet_%C3%A0_d%C3%A9biter_les_lapins_03.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5098" data-file-height="2868" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A <a href = vnd.unilang:cleaver.html>cleaver</a>.</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaver.html>cleaver</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cleavers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A squarish, heavy knife used by <a href = vnd.unilang:butchers.html>butchers</a> for hacking through <a href = vnd.unilang:bones.html>bones</a> etc.
<ul><li><b>1883</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Howard_Pyle" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Howard Pyle">Howard <a href = vnd.unilang:pyle.html>Pyle</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Merry_Adventures_of_Robin_Hood" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Merry Adventures of Robin Hood">The Merry Adventures of <a href = vnd.unilang:robin.html>Robin</a> Hood</a></i> <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Merry_Adventures_of_Robin_Hood/Chapter_V" class="extiw" title="s:The Merry Adventures of Robin Hood/Chapter V">Chapter V</a>
<dl><dd>When he <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to Nottingham, he entered that part of the market where <a href = vnd.unilang:butchers.html>butchers</a> stood, and <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> up his inn in the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> place he could find. Next, he opened his stall and spread his meat upon the bench, then, taking his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaver.html>cleaver</a></b> and steel and clattering them together, he trolled <a href = vnd.unilang:aloud.html>aloud</a> in merry tones:...</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1946</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mervyn_Peake" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mervyn Peake">Mervyn Peake</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Titus_Groan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Titus Groan">Titus Groan</a></i>
<dl><dd>Concurrently with Flay's visualization of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaver.html>cleaver</a></b> falling—the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaver.html>cleaver</a></b> fell.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Bahamas</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A type of clave, or rhythm stick, a concussive musical instrument used in traditional Bahamian music.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metaphoric</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The act of eliminating someone or something, especially when done by someone with a history of other eliminations; a dismissal, rejection, or removal.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b> May 13,  <a href = vnd.unilang:barney.html>Barney</a> Ronay,  “Antonio Conte’s brilliance <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> Chelsea’s pop-up team into champions”, in  <cite>the Guardian</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.theguardian.com/football/blog/2017/may/13/antonio-conte-chelsea-champions-manager">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Conte <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> broken the mould further with the suggestion he might escape the Abramovich <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaver.html>cleaver</a></b>, becoming the first of his line to leave by his own volition.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">axe</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>As a musical instrument, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:cleaver.html>cleaver</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> normally used only in the plural, just like the more common synonym <i>claves</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> far more often used internationally and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> better known as a part of Cuban music. In the Bahamas, <i>cleavers</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the more common terminology.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klibą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href = vnd.unilang:klif.html>klif</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:clif.html>clif</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clef</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klif.html>klif</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">kleb</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:klif.html>klif</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***cliff.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>cliff</a> (5891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">clyf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:clif.html>clif</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klibą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>cliff</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cliffs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A vertical (or nearly vertical) rock face.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">precipice</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hyponym"><span class="defdate">Hyponym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">escarpment</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms coordinate-term"><span class="defdate">Coordinate term:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bluff</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A point where something abruptly fails or decreases in value etc.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>cliff</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cliffs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Obsolete form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">clef</i></span></span>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1723</b>,  John Harris,  <cite>Lexicon Technicum</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Suppose a Person hath learnt to sing in the Treble <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>Cliff</a></b> only, and would sing Notes prick'd in the Tenor <a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>Cliff</a> on the middle <a href = vnd.unilang:tine.html>tine</a> with F <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***clipper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:clipper.html>clipper</a> (65625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">klepper</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">clippen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">clyppan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klupjaną</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/clipper" class="extiw" title="w:clipper"><a href = vnd.unilang:clipper.html>clipper</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/clipper" class="extiw" title="w:clipper">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:clipper.html>clipper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:clippers.html>clippers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Anything that <a href = vnd.unilang:clips.html>clips</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tool used for clipping something, such as hair, coins, or fingernails.</li>
<li>Something that <a href = vnd.unilang:moves.html>moves</a> swiftly; especially:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of several forms of very fast sailing ships having a long, low hull and a sharply raked <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An Alberta <a href = vnd.unilang:clipper.html>clipper</a>.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The Asian butterfly <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parthenos_sylvia" class="extiw" title="w:Parthenos sylvia">Parthenos sylvia</a></i>, family Nymphalidae.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">electronics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A circuit which prevents the amplitude of a wave from exceeding a set value.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person who mutilates coins by fraudulently <a href = vnd.unilang:paring.html>paring</a> the edges.
<ul><li>c. <b>1598</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_V_(play)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry V (play)"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> V</a></i>, Act IV, Scene 1,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/plays/play_view.php?WorkID=henry5amp;Scope=entireamp;pleasewait=1amp;msg=pl">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Indeed, the French may lay twenty French crowns to one, they will beat us; for they bear them on their <a href = vnd.unilang:shoulders.html>shoulders</a>: but it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no English treason to cut French crowns, and to-morrow the king himself will be a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clipper.html>clipper</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1781</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_Brinsley_Sheridan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Richard Brinsley Sheridan">Richard Brinsley Sheridan</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_School_for_Scandal" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The School for Scandal">The School for Scandal</a></i>, London: J. Bew, Act II, p. 21,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/004821556.0001.000">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Many a wretch who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> drawn upon a hurdle, <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> done less mischief than those barterers of forged lies, coiners of scandal, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clippers.html>clippers</a></b> of reputation.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2010</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_K._Morrow" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:James K. Morrow">James Morrow</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Last_Witchfinder" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Last Witchfinder">The Last Witchfinder</a></i>
<dl><dd>Surtouts billowing in an unseasonably fierce wind, the ursine Chelmsford magistrate and his equally bulky constable herded their bound prisoners – three murderers, three <a href = vnd.unilang:thieves.html>thieves</a>, a coin <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clipper.html>clipper</a></b>, two convicted witches – across the Common <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Confidence <a href = vnd.unilang:trickster.html>trickster</a>; conman.
<ul><li><i>1848'</i>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Makepeace_Thackeray" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Makepeace Thackeray">William Makepeace Thackeray</a>, <i>Vanity Fair</i>, Chapter 16:
<dl><dd>"You have head enough for both of us, <a href = vnd.unilang:beck.html>Beck</a>," <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> he. "You're sure to get us out of the scrape. I never saw your equal, and I've <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> with some <b><a href = vnd.unilang:clippers.html>clippers</a></b> in my time too."</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***clive.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:clive.html>clive</a> (9008)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">cliven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">clīfan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a>, adhere, stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klībaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to glue, stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gleybʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lubricate, stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleven.html>kleven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to adhere, stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kleben</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to adhere, stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">kliva</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to climb, stalk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">klífa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to climb, ascend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:clive.html>clive</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">clives</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cliving</b>, <i>simple past</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en">clived</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en">clove</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">clived</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cliven</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To climb; ascend.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">clife</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clifers (cleavers), burdock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleven.html>kleve</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">klijve</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burdock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">klive</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burdock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:clive.html>clive</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">clives</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Burdock or agrimony.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">cliven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">klyfja</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">klufða</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to split, chop, <a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kleubaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to split, pick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*glewbʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut, carve, peel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">clēofan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a>, split, separate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:clive.html>clive</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">clives</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cliving</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">clived</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To split; separate; <a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a>; chop.
<ul><li><b>1990</b>, John Ashurst, Francis G. Dimes, <i>Conservation of building and decorative stone: Volume 1</i>:
<dl><dd>After 'frosting' the stone may be '<b>clived'</b> or split along the bedding <a href = vnd.unilang:planes.html>planes</a>. Once <b>clived</b>, the thin slabs are dressed for use and <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> as Collyweston Slates, for use as tilestones.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2007</b>, Robert <a href = vnd.unilang:ader.html>Ader</a>, <i>Psychoneuroimmunology</i>:
<dl><dd>IL-1β presents the peculiarity of being produced in the form of a biologically inactive precursor, known as ProIL-1β, that needs to be <b>clived</b> at an aspartate residue by a specific enzyme, named interleukin-1β converting enzyme (ICE) or [...]</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***cobweb.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cobweb.html>cobweb</a> (94549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">copweb</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">coppeweb</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cop</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spider</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">web</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kopwebbe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Kobbenwebbe</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Westphalian</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cobweb" class="extiw" title="w:cobweb"><a href = vnd.unilang:cobweb.html>cobweb</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cobweb" class="extiw" title="w:cobweb">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cobweb.html>cobweb</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cobwebs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A spiderweb, or the <a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a> of one, especially an asymmetrical one that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> woven with an irregular pattern of threads.
<ul><li><b>1865</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> David Thoreau, <i>Cape Cod</i>, Chapter X. "Provincetown", page 200.
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="I found him sitting in his front doorway, that Sabbath evening, prepared for me to come in unto him; but unfortunately for his reputation for keeping open house,">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> stretched across his gateway a circular <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cobweb.html>cobweb</a></b> of the largest <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> and quite entire. This looked so ominous that I actually <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> aside and <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> in the back way.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1907</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbara_Baynton" class="extiw" title="w:Barbara Baynton">Barbara Baynton</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sally.html>Sally</a> Krimmer; Alan <a href = vnd.unilang:lawson.html>Lawson</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:editors.html>editors</a>, <cite>Human Toll</cite> (<a href = vnd.unilang:portable.html>Portable</a> Australian Authors: Barbara Baynton), St Lucia |  University of Queensland Press, published 1980, page 286:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cobweb.html>cobweb</a></b>, night-spun, hung in an insidious circle from branch to branch, facing her. Early as it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, its first victim struggled in its gummy meshes.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>One of its filaments; gossamer</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something thin and unsubstantial, or flimsy and worthless; valueless remainder.
<ul><li><b>c. 1579</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philip_Sidney" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Philip Sidney">Philip <a href = vnd.unilang:sidney.html>Sidney</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Defense_of_Poesy" class="extiw" title="s:The Defense of Poesy">The Defense of Poesy</a></i>
<dl><dd>The dust and <b>cobwebs</b> of that uncivil age.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b> February 10,  <a href = vnd.unilang:phil.html>Phil</a> McNulty,  “Tottenham Hotspur 1 <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> 0 Arsenal”, in  <cite>BBC</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.bbc.com/sport/football/42927831">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Once the <b>cobwebs</b> of a lack-lustre first <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> blown away, <a href = vnd.unilang:spurs.html>Spurs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> irresistible and Arsenal <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> simply unable to cope with the power of Mousa Dembele in midfield and the creation and running of Christian Eriksen and <a href = vnd.unilang:dele.html>Dele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alli.html>Alli</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> combined with the inevitable goalscoring prowess of <a href = vnd.unilang:kane.html>Kane</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>An intricate plot to catch the unwary
<ul><li><b>1785</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Cowper" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Cowper">William Cowper</a>, <i>The Task</i>
<dl><dd>Entangled in the <b>cobwebs</b> of the schools.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Internet <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A web page that either <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> not <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> updated for a long time, or that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> rarely visited</li>
<li>The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_spotted_flycatcher" class="extiw" title="w:European spotted flycatcher">European spotted flycatcher</a>, <i>Muscicapa striata</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fuzzy inexact memories
<ul><li><b>2008</b> Burlan Eugene Ellison <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=6WHcBAAAQBAJamp;pg=PA98">The <a href = vnd.unilang:ebony.html>Ebony</a> Coffin: A <a href = vnd.unilang:jim.html>Jim</a> Kirkwood Novel</a> page 98
<dl><dd>I washed my face, trying to get the <b>cobwebs</b> of hard sex and an alcohol-induced sleep out of my head</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2012</b> Stanley M. Bierman <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=lh1BtACaOGYCamp;pg=PA16"><a href = vnd.unilang:napoleon.html>Napoleon</a>'s <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>Penis</a>: Plus Other Engaging and Outrageous Tales</a> page 16
<dl><dd>Veyz rnir, meaning something like “Oh . . . my!,” <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a Yiddish expression that I <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> not employed for a long, long time. Yet in the <b>cobwebs</b> of my memory, that expression <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> still lurking inside. How interesting!</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2019</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.springfieldspringfield.co.uk/view_episode_scripts.php?tv-show=empire-2015amp;episode=s05e13">Hot Blood, Hot Thoughts, Hot <a href = vnd.unilang:deeds.html>Deeds</a></a>, <i>Empire</i> season 5 episode 13
<dl><dd>I'm just saying, you being a <a href = vnd.unilang:mama.html>mama</a>, it's time to clear the <b>cobwebs</b>. You know what I'm saying? Put a banana in the monkey. You know, hot dog in your bun.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
